Editorial

Two Inexplicable Things 29

Perhaps because the weather is hot, people are psychologically irritable. In addition, many things at home and abroad are often unexpected. Therefore, the news reported in the past few days often makes ordinary people incomprehensible. Let's take two things to prove my point. But we still hope that everyone can calm down, restore their senses, and not let their emotions run wild and their minds be frightened, which will only make national affairs worse.

First, what we find most strange is that Mr. Zhou Enlai openly stated in his speech to reporters in Shanghai the day before yesterday that Mr. Chen Lifu's mission to Shanghai was to "strengthen secret agents and arrange new political assassinations." He even falsely accused that "the names of many democratic people are already on the black list, and their lives are already in Mr. Chen's hands, so the Kunming incident can happen at any time in Beijing, Shanghai and other places." This kind of statement from the mouth of the leader of the Communist Party is not only a faux pas, but simply violates criminal law. Announcing this publicly to 60 or 70 Chinese and foreign reporters, no wonder Mr. Chen wants to send a letter to question Mr. Zhou and ask him to bear the legal responsibility for insults and defamation. But why is Mr. Zhou's emotions so agitated? Thinking about it, it is incomprehensible. Some people believe that from the recent secret documents of the Chinese Communist Party, it can be seen that they are arranging to create massacres in various places. Is Mr. Zhou saying these words because they themselves want to do it, sacrifice a few "democratic people" who have already been used, and then use them as an excuse to attack the government? According to the Chinese Communist Party's doctrine that "everyone is a tool and everything is a process," and the Chinese Communist Party's past practice of shouting that others are going to attack before they do, it may be possible to infer that this is the case. But judging from human nature, we are still unwilling to believe it and dare not believe it. Because if the Chinese Communist Party really does this, everyone will only provide them with tools. Who else would be willing to be friends with them in good faith? Therefore, after hearing Zhou Enlai's emotionally激越 (stirring) speech, we still don't understand what he really meant.

Second, what we also find strange is the rash action of LaGuardia, the director of the "United Nations Relief and Rehabilitation Administration" (UNRRA), to suspend the transportation of materials to China. UNRRA is an organization jointly organized by various countries, and China is a major participating country. Everyone knows that China's eight years of resistance against Japan is in dire need of relief. Why did UNRRA lightly believe the false reports of some people in the China Branch and take such a reckless action? What is especially ridiculous is that LaGuardia himself has not even figured out the names, positions, and nationalities of the 225 people who filed the complaint, and suddenly issued this unexpected order based on his personal subjectivity! Recently, we heard a responsible senior official say that UNRRA used to supply many Chinese people with unnecessary materials, and even "fake goods" and "bad goods" were mixed in. We don't understand why UNRRA doesn't conduct a thorough investigation itself first? Moreover, UNRRA ships materials to China ship by ship without consulting China's opinions in advance, nor notifying the Chinese government. When the ship arrives at the port, it still can't produce a manifest. There is actually such a relief agency in the world. How can we blame people for distributing it slowly? As for whether it is necessary for so many foreign friends from the "UNRRA" branch in China to come to China batch by batch, let alone say, they must first take care of their food and lodging before participating in China's political role, colluding with the Chinese Communist Party from the inside and outside, and destroying the unity of China's administrative system. Is this really the original intention of relief? We think about it, think about it, and can't figure out why these foreign friends from "UNRRA" want to do this? LaGuardia said that he didn't like any foreigner, but he was hired by President Song because of his love affair. Could it be that he can make things difficult for the Chinese people who are being relieved because of this bit of spite? What is even more incomprehensible is that the "UNRRA" in China has been so corrupt in the past, the "UNRRA" has insulted China so much, and this part of the foreigners in the "UNRRA branch" has reported so recklessly, but the director of our "Executive Yuan Relief and Rehabilitation Administration" (行總) didn't know anything about it beforehand? If he knew, why didn't he report it to the government and the society? Why didn't he explain the truth to various countries in advance? Why didn't he argue according to reason at the Far East Commission meeting afterwards, but instead agreed with the opinions of the representatives of other countries, thinking that LaGuardia's policy was not entirely wrong? Some people also said that Director Jiang is wholeheartedly dealing with more important matters these days, so no wonder him. If so, what else can we say!

Correspondences from Various Places 30

The Huai River Rises and Floods

Affecting the Reconstruction of the Huai River Embankment; Bengbu City Intensifies Flood Prevention

[Our newspaper, Bengbu Correspondence] Anhui Province is now in the major flood season. The clouds and rain are transporting cotton. The water levels of the Huai River upstream and downstream are rising continuously, which has greatly affected the reconstruction of the Huai River embankment undertaken by the Guidance Committee. The section from the Over-the-River Mouth on the left bank of the Huai River to Shaojia Avenue is basically completed, with a total length of 29.8 kilometers. The section from Zhengyangguan to Sanhejian cannot be constructed due to the overflowing river water, and has been temporarily suspended. A part of the Huai River embankment in Fengtai has been forced to stop construction due to the surging floods, but a part is still being processed and rushed to repair. Although the embankment from Huaiyuan to Linhuai has not been fully completed, the built embankment has reached the high level of major floodwaters. It can be used for flood prevention and will not overflow. However, the water level of the Huai River has been rising continuously in recent days. According to the observation report here on the 15th: the Huai River water level in Bengbu was 18.81 meters at 7:00 a.m., 18.82 meters at 1:00 p.m., and 18.825 meters at 7:00 p.m. If it continues to rise, the Huai River embankment may inevitably be submerged. The flood prevention agencies in Bengbu City have intensified prevention.

Meeting of the Standing Committee of the Provisional参议会 (Provisional People's Council) of Fengxian County

The Provisional参议会 (Provisional People's Council) of this county held a meeting of the Standing Committee at 3:00 p.m. on the 16th. The head of the County Land and Food Department was invited to attend. The meeting was chaired by Speaker He to discuss the issue of grain requisition in this year's land tax. Considering that the main agricultural products of this county are cotton and wool (70% cotton and 30% rice), all grain requisition in this county should be based on the standard of 70% cotton and 30% rice to show fairness and relieve the people's difficulties. It was decided that the council would submit a special report to the higher authorities for adoption, and compile statistics on the annual crop yields, grain tax, and rural economic situation of this county for provincial reference.

Soldier of the Songjiang Jinshan Team Executed for Drug Trafficking

Jiang Caihe, a soldier of the Jinshan County Security Team, was arrested by the Songjiang Water Police Headquarters in Mishidu for trafficking in heroin. A large bag of heroin was found on the spot. He was immediately escorted to the Third District Security Command for interrogation. Later, the prisoner confessed to drug trafficking without denial. He was sentenced to death according to law. At noon on the 18th, the unit took the prisoner to Yanjiatan, Maluqiao to verify his identity and execute him by shooting.

Changshu County Government Thoroughly Investigates Two Cases of Malpractice

The two major malpractice cases of the County Tenant Rent Committee and the Hupu Branch of the Autonomous Tax Department have been thoroughly investigated separately for severe punishment. Yan Shen, the former director of the Tenant Rent Committee, was decided by the Provisional参议会 (Provisional People's Council) to be escorted for handling, and the county magistrate immediately ordered his arrest at the police station. Gu Xia, the director of the Hupu Branch of the Tax Department, abused his power for personal gain and altered tax tickets. After the county government sent personnel to investigate and verify the facts, it ordered an investigation. Magistrate Pan also stated at the morning meeting that malpractices by tax personnel must be punished and will not be tolerated.

Wuxi River Water Has Receded and Rice Prices Have Fallen

In early this month, there were several days of heavy rain in the county, and the river water rose by two feet. Low-lying fields were about to become marshes, and farmers were extremely anxious. The weather was clear with strong winds, and the river water has receded. The danger of low-lying fields has been lifted. On the 17th, the market price of white rice fell. High-quality white japonica rice was 56,000 yuan per stone, japonica rice was 23,500 yuan, and foreign indica rice was 21,000 yuan. The prices of other items such as Du wheat, foreign wheat, warship brand flour, and southern river soybeans also fell.

Stalin Intensifies Purge of the Military; Reorganization of the Soviet High Command; Wartime Hero Zhukov Demoted 31

[Our Own Dispatch] London, 19th (Broadcast): The highest Soviet authorities have implemented a military purge. Georgy Zhukov, the commander of the Soviet forces that captured Berlin, has been transferred to a less important military post. Furthermore, other highly prominent military leaders have been dismissed. The purpose of the purge is to eliminate pro-British and American elements. The British side is paying close attention to this.

[United Press, New York, 18th] Stalin has implemented a purge among high-ranking military officers, demoting General Georgy Zhukov, the Soviet Union's number one wartime hero, to a regional commander. While no official announcement has been made regarding the reorganization, it is understood that such a reorganization is already underway. So far, the main casualty known is Zhukov, who was transferred to the post of Commander of Soviet Ground Forces three months ago and also elevated to membership in the Presidium of the Supreme Soviet. He is now being transferred to the Odessa Military District. It is rumored that Zhukov is not the only casualty of this reorganization. However, no other changes are yet known. It is rumored that, in essence, this military purge is already underway, although not as severe as the 1937 purge, when high-ranking Red Army officers were all dismissed and accused of collaborating with Trotsky and other political enemies, and subjected to the death penalty. Zhukov's demotion does not seem to be due to differences in political views, but rather suspicion of disloyalty to the country. While serving as the Soviet representative to the Allied Control Council in Berlin, he became a friend of Eisenhower. The successor to the post of Commander of Soviet Ground Forces has not yet been announced. He remains a member of the Politburo, the highest organ of the Soviet Communist Party. The Odessa Military District is in charge of southern Russia and the Balkan border area. Before the war, Odessa was an important military district in western Russia. The Red Army newspaper "Red Star" recently launched a major propaganda campaign to rectify Red Army discipline, with particular emphasis on the security of the Soviet Union.

Under the European "Iron Curtain"; Britain Pursues Dual Diplomacy; On One Hand, Considers Granting the Soviets Huge Loans to Restore Trade; On the Other Hand, Agrees with the US to Unify the German Economy 32

[Agence France-Presse, London, 18th] Whether the European "Iron Curtain" can be lifted, or whether it will deepen further, will be known within a few days. Well-informed sources have recently said that the British government is holding talks with the Soviet Union in London, while also conducting negotiations with the United States in Berlin, hoping to improve the current situation. Britain now has two paths to follow: one is to strive to establish a closer relationship with the Soviet Union, and the other is to stand in opposition to the Soviet Union and divide Germany in two, thereby dividing Europe and even the entire world. Regarding this matter, the British Minister of Commerce, Cripps, is currently in London negotiating with the Soviet representative, Kransov, preparing to establish a commercial agreement as a basis for clarifying the general relationship between the two sides. In addition, British representatives are also in Berlin holding talks with the US side, hoping to prepare for the economic unification of Germany in the British, American, and French occupation zones. If the Soviet Union does not fully agree, it will be implemented regardless of Soviet objections. The above two talks are taking place in secret, but according to reliable sources, since last year, commercial relations between Britain and the Soviet Union have been interrupted due to the Soviet side's refusal to allow the import of British goods. These goods are worth about 11 million pounds and are ready for shipment. As of the end of April this year, about 140 British manufacturers, including the automobile and textile industries, have suggested to the British Ministry of Commerce and Supply that they plan to restore commerce with the Soviet Union and grant the Soviet Union a 50 million pound credit loan for a term of ten years. The talks currently underway in London are based on this suggestion. However, the Soviet side believes that the value of the various goods is too high and has not agreed to accept them. Fortunately, the Soviet Union has transported a large number of gold bars into Britain, which may serve as a guarantee for the ten-year credit loan. As for the talks being conducted by British and American experts in Berlin, their primary goal is to separate the eastern and western parts of Germany. The main points are: (1) The UK and the US should make full use of all assets in their occupation zones and should not import goods from the Soviet Union; (2) The UK and the US subcommittees should formulate plans for their respective occupation zones to encourage production and determine prices; (3) If the UK and the US are unable to reach an agreement with the Soviet Union, they should mutually agree on price levels and use the Mark as an exchange tool; (4) When the talks reach the final stage, France should be invited to participate. To this end, well-informed sources concluded that the talks currently underway in London are quite optimistic and seem to want to establish a reasonable agreement. The talks being conducted in Berlin, on the other hand, could separate Western Europe from Eastern Europe. Their nature is completely different.

Atomic Bomb Test Exercise; Explodes Fifty Minutes Earlier Than Scheduled; Power Equivalent to 400,000 Depth Charges 34

[Our Own Dispatch] San Francisco, 19th (Broadcast): During the atomic bomb exercise held on Bikini Atoll today, the dummy bomb, a magnesium flash bomb, exploded suddenly fifty-one minutes before the scheduled time. Although the premature explosion and bad weather forced most of the aircraft to return to base, another dummy bomb exploded at the specified time, and the exercise was not disrupted. According to Blandy, the cause of the premature explosion is unknown. According to the explanation of staff officers, it was caused by an error in the electrical circuitry, and it suddenly exploded at 8:14 AM. Blandy said that the premature explosion has little to do with the actual atomic bomb test, because the electrical circuit for initiating the bomb was not adequately protected. He also said that when conducting the real underwater atomic bomb explosion, the accuracy of the explosion time is guaranteed. When the magnesium flash bomb exploded, a violent shock occurred in the air above, and forty-seven aircraft participating in the exercise were forced to retreat, leaving only nine to observe the weather.

[Special Dispatch from Central News Agency Reporter Song Dehe aboard the USS Appalachian en route to Bikini, 18th] The second atomic bomb test at Bikini, as far as the reporter is concerned, will be more spectacular and more dramatic than the one held on July 1st. According to the current plan, when the atomic bomb is tested on the 25th of this month, the reporter will be able to observe it from a closer location. This explosion is expected to inflict greater damage on the target ships. US Navy officials today told reporters that this second atomic bomb test will be an underwater explosion. It is estimated that its impact on the ships will be four times stronger than the previous air explosion. According to their rough estimate, the atomic bomb exploded on that day will be equivalent to 400,000 depth charges. It is understood that the test bomb will be placed between 18 feet below the surface of the water and the bottom of the lagoon (about 120 feet). This fifth atomic bomb placed underwater will be like an underwater-controlled mine.

[United Press dispatch from the USS Appalachian, the viewing ship for the atomic bomb test, 18th] On the 25th of this month, its mechanism is based on the speed of sound. This speed is about every five seconds in the air; but in the lagoon it is about two miles per second. Vibrations in the water and lagoon travel at the same extraordinary speed as the explosion. The bomb's entire atomic energy enters the water, and just as an aerial explosion dissipates into the air, the Bikini coral reef may suffer a catastrophe. But not all of the atomic energy enters the Bikini water. The exact proportion is a military secret and a point of contention among scientists. These vibrations are expected to touch the bottom of the Bikini coral reef.

The Soviets Send More Personnel to Observe the Test

[United Press reporter's special dispatch from a ship en route to Bikini] In addition to the two scientists previously designated, the Soviet Union has added one more person, Lieutenant Commander Kokarov, as a "news representative" to observe the underwater explosion test of the atomic bomb at Bikini. With the exception of the United Kingdom, all other invited countries have sent two people. China has also sent two scientists to participate.

Secret Weapons Manufacturing Plant; Suspects Fired

This is still in accordance with the Army National Defense Regulations. Cripps Reports on His Mission to India in the British House of Commons; He Met with Representatives of Various Indian Factions with Sincerity; Helping Them Narrow Their Differences and Complete the Constitution as Soon as Possible 40

[Reuters, London, 18th] Cripps, one of the British cabinet representatives to India, recently stated in the House of Commons that the situation of this cabinet delegation to India was very different from when he was ordered to go to India in 1942. He said that the whole world is now politically aware, and so are the people of India. The House of Commons should know that the situation in the spring of 1946 is very different from that in 1942 or 1939. India is now deeply politically aware after the war, and the pressure that could be applied before the war is no longer appropriate. The steadfastness of delegation leader Lawrence in handling negotiations in India is commendable and has led to the current outcome. Some people criticize our talks as a waste of time, but in fact, this is very valuable to our mission. Contacting the various factions of 400 million Indians is very helpful in determining the direction of negotiations. We are not overly optimistic about the agreement reached at the round table conference held by the delegation with the Muslim League and the Congress Party in Simla. In Simla, we failed to bring them closer, and the meeting ended after two weeks. We returned to New Delhi and announced our views. We did indeed make every effort in Simla to generate a plan suitable for negotiation, so that we were able to issue a statement on May 16 after returning to New Delhi. Although we failed to announce a plan to prove our identity as the Indians had hoped, the purpose of our trip was not to implement a plan on India, but to help the Indians reach an agreement among themselves. We do not want to interfere in the organization of India's future constitution, but want to invite representatives of various factions in India to organize a constitutional assembly to discuss major plans together, because this is entirely a matter for the Indians themselves. Therefore, our basic policy is only to make suggestions to enable Indians to reach an agreement themselves and organize a constitutional assembly. That is why. This suggestion has been highly praised by all parties. Before we left India, representatives of all parties expressed their desire to promote the work of the constitutional assembly and provided suggestions on how to make it work, but it must be based on the conditions of the May 16 statement in order not to harm the interests of other relevant parties.

Without large-scale aid from Britain, France was unable to fight Germany. Crossing the Illinois Prairie: A Visit to President Lincoln's Hometown - Scenes Remain Unchanged, as if Stepping Back a Century 48

— Special Correspondent in the United States, Mao Shuqing (Concluded)

Hall, Lincoln's predecessor as postmaster, came from New Jersey. After resigning from the post office, he built a "two-story" wooden house and set up a small store selling various groceries. It is said that Hall was a rather "important" figure in New Salem Village at the time. After Lincoln resigned as postmaster, he followed Hall's path and opened a "Lincoln Grocery Store." The Lincoln Grocery Store was built under a large locust tree and was the last of the dozen or so humble houses in the village to be built. In front of the door was a dirt road, and presumably muddy and slippery on rainy days, Lincoln paved a few scattered stones, but the stones were very smooth. I worry that Lincoln must have fallen on rainy days.

The Lincoln Grocery Store contains various simple daily necessities from the United States a hundred years ago, as well as woodwork made by Lincoln himself. Opposite the grocery store is Lincoln's home. Lincoln married and had children in the village in 1842, which can be seen in Lincoln's letters. One of Lincoln's children died young in that village. In Lincoln's so-called "home," there is a "grandfather clock," a kitchen, and a very simple fireplace for heating in winter. There are also several double-decker beds, which every family in the village has. The tour guide said: Parents sleep on the upper bunk, and babies sleep on the lower bunk. There were two doctors in the village, and the doctor's house was slightly more "spacious." Later, after Lincoln was elected president, the doctor moved away from the village. The United States is a very young country, but the people of the young country also "yearn for the past." Their enthusiasm for yearning for the past is admirable, and they want to maintain the "realism" of the objects, which is rare in other countries. Only one house in the entire village is modern, and that is the Lincoln Memorial Museum. The museum displays letters that Lincoln sent to his family elders, written from the White House after Lincoln was elected president. The letters contain many words of nostalgia for that small village. In addition, there are weapons used by the assassin who murdered President Lincoln, and digging tools and hammers used by traitors who later attempted to steal Lincoln's body. Also on display is the piano used by Lincoln at his wedding, as well as books with Lincoln's handwritten annotations. Lincoln lived in New Salem Village for six years before moving to Springfield. That was after Lincoln's marriage. There is a so-called Lincoln Home in Springfield, which is the second noteworthy place I want to talk about. It is a modern Western-style house, not far from the current Illinois State Capitol. It is now managed by the state government as a park, surrounded by white walls. Lincoln's house is on a street corner, bordering roads on both sides. The house has two floors, and there is a very small garden in the back. The house is white, and the window sills are green. There are five rooms inside. The upstairs is not open to the public. There is a government administrator downstairs. Visitors must write down their names and resumes before entering. The first room is a parlor, with an old sofa. The administrator said: That was Mrs. Lincoln's sitting room. Although old, it is incomparable to the humble farmhouses in New Salem Village. In Lincoln's study, there is a Mobil kerosene lamp, oil paintings and vases, an old-fashioned fireplace, a child's seat, and the silk that Lincoln once used. Lincoln lived in this house for seventeen years (1844-1861), so it is called "Lincoln's Home." On the door of the house, there are two bronze plaques. One says "Lincoln's Home," and the other contains a poem by Vachel Lindsay, describing Lincoln's tall, thin figure, how he entered and exited this house, and describing a large group of children playing in front of the door. This poem is very famous in the United States, excerpted from Lindsay's "Abraham Lincoln Walks at Midnight." The Illinois government has grand notices in New Salem Village and the "Lincoln's Home" in the city, preserving the antique charm, and inserting large American flags. The number of stars on the flag is different, representing how many states the United States had at that time. After seeing the Lincoln Home, it seems like we have returned to after 1861. Lincoln was elected president, and the North-South war broke out to liberate black slaves. After four years of fighting, Lincoln succeeded and died. Lincoln was assassinated by rebel forces in 1865 and transported back to Springfield for burial. Lincoln's physical body died, but Lincoln's spirit lives on forever! No one does not admire Lincoln's greatness, especially after you visit Lincoln's tomb. The tomb's architecture is very simple and solemn, all made of granite. The burial chamber is under the granite. Visitors can enter after signing their names. On the walls of the burial chamber are Lincoln's writings, proclamations, and the most famous Gettysburg Address of November 19, 1863. In the center of the burial chamber is Lincoln's coffin, on which is written "Now he belongs to the ages." On the stone wall in front of the burial chamber are engraved the names of Lincoln's family and their dates of birth and death. The cemetery is near the suburbs of Springfield. From afar, you can see large lawns, green shade, and the tall granite tomb tower. The names of the forty-eight states are engraved around the tomb tower, and bronze statues are installed at the four corners, all in the uniforms of soldiers from the North-South War era; infantry, artillery, and other unnamed martyrs, these people followed President Lincoln and laid the national foundation for the United States. A large bronze statue of President Lincoln stands in front of the tomb. Every day, many American men and women come from all directions to pay their respects to Lincoln, the most outstanding figure of their history. The Lincoln Cemetery is also a public cemetery. All around are filled tombs, which are the American people who have died. Lincoln's impression on the American people is profound. Without Lincoln, the unification of the United States would not have been established so completely; without Lincoln, the industrialization of the United States might have been delayed for decades. The Civil War was not Lincoln's goal. Lincoln's contribution to the United States was a strong unified state, and accelerated industrialization. These two magic weapons were precisely the important factors that the United States later used to defeat Spain, defeat Germany twice, and defeat Japan once. Lincoln laid an unshakeable foundation for the United States' current position as a world leader. Who says President Lincoln has died? Lincoln is living forever! (Sent from Jacksonville, Illinois)

Lincoln's Grocery Store (Sent by Special Correspondent Mao Shuqing)

Page 4

He DeKui Responds to the Case of Senator Wu Yifang's Accusation: Asks Himself if His Actions Are Upright and Open, Regarding His Relationship with the Enemy and Puppets 49

[Report from this newspaper] When the Standing Committee of the National Senate of Nanjing held its regular meeting yesterday morning, Standing Committee Member Ms. Wu Yifang (President of Jinling Women's University) accused He DeKui, the current Secretary-General of the Shanghai Municipal Government, of being a suspected traitor, and said that she had photos as evidence. All sectors of the city were shocked upon hearing the news. At 5 p.m. yesterday, reporters from various newspapers went to the municipal government to interview Secretary-General He DeKui. At that time, He had just returned from the review meeting of the Relief and Rehabilitation Administration. He immediately received the reporters in the conference room of the municipal government. He, wearing a white summer cloth long shirt and holding a black paper fan, was very calm. He smiled and told the reporters: Regarding the transmission of this unexpected news, I would like to state three facts: (1) After the Pearl Harbor Incident on December 8, 1941, the British and American General Manager, directors, director-general, head of the finance department, and staff of all ranks of the Shanghai Municipal Council continued to serve in the Municipal Council in accordance with the intentions of the US authorities. Therefore, I should also continue to serve. (2) I served in the Municipal Council with the British and Americans. The Japanese enemy did not appoint the retained British and Americans, nor did they appoint DeKui and others, because the Municipal Council was an international organization. (3) Later, rumors spread that the puppet regime in Nanjing was going to take over the Shanghai Municipal Council. I immediately resigned. Therefore, when the traitor Chen Gongbo came to take over, I had already left. At that time, the enemy and puppets tried their best to win me over, but I refused them all. Therefore, my actions were upright and open. I would also like to state that I have never belonged to any party or faction. During the Shanghai Municipal Council era, on June 1, 1932, I was recommended by the Chinese directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council to serve as a co-manager. After six years, I was promoted to deputy director-general, also for nearly six years. During the period of the city's occupation, I only served as a consultant to Chinese commercial and industrial circles, such as banks and spinning mills, to earn a living. After the restoration, I served as the chairman of the Committee for the United Allied Forces Reception of Compatriots in Concentration Camps of the Three People's Principles Youth League, as well as a member of the Shanghai Municipal Real Estate Management Committee, deputy director of the Housing Rental Management Committee, and deputy mayor of Shanghai. Later, the deputy mayor system was abolished, so I was renamed Secretary-General. For more than ten years, I have been dedicated to my duty, law-abiding, and clean, without any hypocrisy. However, I may occasionally offend people due to official duties, but all of them are for the public good, without any personal prejudice.

He then told the reporters about the joke made by the square weekly "Jeep," saying that a few months ago, "Jeep" published a news item that "Deputy Mayor He tried his best to protect Ding Jiwan." For a while, rumors abounded, and some people even reported to Chairman Chiang, the Executive Yuan, and the Control Yuan. In fact, there was no basis at all, and the publication immediately published a correction in the next issue after the incident. The unfounded rumors also broke down on their own. Therefore, he said that he did not take the news of being accused of being a suspected traitor very seriously, and said that it could be verified by the facts.

He also said: He and Wu Yifang were not familiar with each other. Before August 13, they met once on a ship, and he had a very good impression of her, and he believed that Wu Yifang would not have any ill feelings towards him. This accusation was probably instigated by others. As for the report that there were photos as evidence, he had no idea and could not guess. During the occupation period, he maintained contact with the central government all along. Yu Bingjian, the current director of the Shanghai Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, knew very well about the patriotic work he did. Moreover, he had never left Shanghai for more than ten years. His every move was known to Chinese and foreigners in Shanghai, so there was no need to repeat them.

According to reports, He is from Jinhua, Zhejiang Province. He studied at Peking University and was at the top of his class. In 1917, he was sent to the United States for further study, ranking first in the Ministry of Education's examination. In 1919, he obtained a bachelor's degree from the University of Wisconsin, and in 1921, he obtained a master's degree in business administration from Harvard University. After returning to China, he served as a professor at Shanghai Datong University and Nanyang University, director of the business department of Guanghua University, and English secretary of the Economic Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Council and the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association. He studied the Shanghai Municipal Council for many years. Therefore, the board of directors of the Municipal Council decided to unanimously approve his appointment as co-manager. He's involvement in commercial and industrial circles began after the occupation. During that time, he once assisted the Xinwen Bao newspaper in handling student loans for the poor. Later, he heard that the traitor Chen Riping was going to join the Xinwen Bao, so he immediately resigned.

Zhang Zhiben Talks About Investigation and Reception Work: Welcomes the People's Secret Reports but Requires Listing Facts - Those Who Violate the Law and Neglect Their Duties Will Be Dealt with Impartially 50

Zhang Zhiben, the head of the Investigation Team for the Reception Work in the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Regions, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing on the morning of the 18th. Yesterday, he received reporters from the Central News Agency at his private residence and said: This team is composed of the Central Supervisory Committee, the Control Yuan, and the National Senate. In order to facilitate the investigation work, it is now divided into three groups: Shanghai-Hangzhou, Nanjing, and Anhui. The Beijing-Shanghai group is responsible for me and Cheng Zhongxing, Fan Zhengbo, Wu Wangji, and Secretary Xu Longchuan. Cheng and Fan are both in Shanghai. Wu and Xu will also come here in a few days and can start work. The location of the team's office has been temporarily decided to be at the Jiangsu Supervisory Commissioner's Office. The working period is set at fifty days. The Shanghai reception work began in August of last year. It has been a year in the blink of an eye. To investigate the reception work of one year in fifty days, the time is very tight. In addition, the enemy and puppet property reception work in the Shanghai area is the most complicated. Therefore, we must take the most economical and effective steps to actively handle it. We hope that the city's party and government agencies, mass organizations, and the press will contact this team to assist in the investigation and provide specific materials for this team to refer to. At the same time, this team hopes to have not only a "radio receiver" but also a "radio transmitter" so that it can publicize the materials to the people of the country at any time after the investigation work begins. This point really depends on the assistance of the press. When reporters asked Zhang whether he accepted the people's "secret reports," he said: "Secret reports" are naturally very good, but the "secret reporters" need to have a responsible spirit. It is said that in the past, the city set up secret report boxes. Among the "secret report" letters received, there were actually names such as "People from the Southeast, Northwest, East, and West" and "A Member of the Nation," and the content of the secret reports often attacked individuals and could not provide correct evidence, which would inevitably lose the meaning of "secret reports." In the future, if there are secret report letters that list the facts and are responsibly signed, this team will welcome them very much.

Talking about the past reception of enemy and puppet property in Shanghai, Zhang said, "I have indeed heard some rumors, and there are many accusations about 'receiving materials' and 'losing people's hearts.' It is also said that there are some edible and usable materials in the warehouse that are being watched to rot without being processed. They only know how to 'receive materials' but do not know how to 'use materials.' All of these are manifestations of dereliction of duty. This team will thoroughly investigate them. If there are situations of abusing power, violating the law, neglecting duties, or being negligent in handling, as long as there is correct proof, this team will deal with them impartially, just like a judge trying a case. If the plaintiff submits evidence, the judge can make a judgment based on the articles of law, without any difficulty."

Regarding how to eliminate corruption, Zhang said: "Corruption is naturally a bad phenomenon, but on the one hand, we shout loudly that 'civil servants cannot live,' and on the other hand, we say that 'civil servants are corrupt,' which is somewhat contradictory. I think that corrupt people are ultimately a minority. We cannot universally apply this kind of 'shameful name' to civil servants, so that those who cherish their own reputation will also have a sense of black and white being difficult to distinguish, leading to a general psychology of 'good people do not become civil servants' and 'civil servants must be corrupt.' It must be known that the country has its own laws to punish those who are truly corrupt and neglect their duties. Just submit the evidence, and the government will punish them immediately. We should not make general accusations, which will only cause suspicion among foreign friends. We must correct this kind of concept. As for the improvement of the treatment of civil servants, it is also an urgent task at hand."

At this time of rampant epidemics, the Shanghai Epidemic Hospital has exhausted the 20 million yuan it previously raised. During the epidemic season of summer and autumn every year, it suspends the diagnosis of ordinary diseases and specializes in treating cholera, dysentery, and other epidemic diseases, day and night, regardless of the poor or the rich, providing diagnosis and medicine free of charge. For poor patients who need to be hospitalized for medical treatment, the required medicine and meals are also free of charge, and the number of free beds is expanded as much as possible to accommodate the poor and sick. In addition to the special, first-class, and second-class wards that charge fees, 100 third-class beds and outpatient medicine are completely free. Now, the cost of medicine is high, and all expenses require 3 million yuan per day. In order to raise funds to provide relief, from the 25th and 26th of this month, they will perform Peking Opera on the Jiancheng Radio Station (call sign XGSH, frequency 840) from 10:00 a.m. to 12:00 p.m., and on the 27th, they will broadcast comic Shanghai Opera and Yue Opera on the Minsheng Radio Station (call sign XPOC, frequency 1040), and on the 28th, they will broadcast on the Jianshe Radio Station (call sign XACS, frequency 940) from 10:00 a.m. to 12:00 p.m. It is hoped that people from all walks of life will be generous in donating money to benefit the patients, so that not only can the epidemic be curbed, but society can also avoid the danger of spreading. It was submitted to the joint meeting of directors and supervisors of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce for discussion and approval, and then submitted to the Standing Committee, the Supreme National Defense Conference of the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, and the two financial and economic departments for adoption and implementation.

Therefore, the content of the plan is humble and without lofty arguments. All the points mentioned are what the government can and should do. Our New Fleet Returns: Sails for Nanjing from Shanghai This Morning; Moored at Wusongkou Yesterday to Load Supplies 53

[Report from Our Newspaper] The eight warships gifted to us by the United States, carrying several hundred Chinese naval officers and soldiers who received training in the U.S., arrived at Wusongkou at dawn yesterday. Reporters and others rushed to the Coastal Defense Command Post of the Taiwan Garrison at Wusongkou at dawn. However, upon our return this time, we swept a mine in Tokyo Bay and the Pacific Ocean, as a token of our desire. After leaving the United States last August, we went to the U.S. naval base in Cuba (Guantanamo) for sea trials and exercises. The famous Missouri and Roosevelt warships often participated in the exercises together. We stayed there for a total of three months. Until October 6th of last year, we again visited overseas Chinese in San Diego on the west coast of the United States. Their enthusiasm truly made us feel ashamed! Later, we also visited the local situations in Zhanba and Mexico City, and were inspected by their authorities. Then we went back to the west coast of the United States to repair the ships, and then transferred to Pearl Harbor to load supplies, passing through Honolulu, Midway Island, and other places before heading to Japan. We stayed in Yokosuka for three days before returning to Shanghai."

The eight warships were lined up in a straight line outside Wusongkou. When the reporters were inspecting them, the warships slowly advanced, with a gentle breeze and slight waves, stretching out endlessly. Lieutenant Colonel Lin Yun also accepted the reporter's photography on the warship. It is reported that Mr. Lin will lead the fleet to Nanjing at 4:00 AM this morning, and will return to Shanghai around the 24th.

As for living allowances, the soldiers received about 30 to 60 U.S. dollars per month. Future treatments have not been fully determined.

As for the number of officers on each warship, there are approximately eight officers and one hundred soldiers. They are all energetic and physically strong and will be the new force of the Chinese navy!

Rules for Managing Restaurants in This City Revised and Passed; Penalties for Tax Evasion and Banquet Levies Re-Established 54

[Report from Our Newspaper] Yesterday, the Municipal Council revised and passed 23 articles of the rules for managing restaurants in this city. The main points are as follows: (1) The scope of management includes hotels, Western restaurants, tea houses, Chinese-style wine shops for on-site consumption, beer for consumption inside and outside the premises, foreign liquor for off-site consumption, temporary bars, Western-style hotels, coffee rooms, noodle shops, dim sum shops, and places that sell food and beverages in public entertainment venues and hotels. (2) Anyone opening a restaurant must obtain a permit according to the procedures before opening. Those established before the promulgation of these rules should apply for the procedures within one month after the promulgation of these rules. (3) The permits are renewed once a year, and the permit will be revoked if the business has not started within one month of obtaining the permit. (4) Restaurants should have appropriate facilities for garbage disposal and drainage, wire mesh disinfection, and stoves should not be installed in the store. (5) Employees and shop assistants must undergo a physical examination once a year.

The Municipal Finance Bureau discovered that banquet hall merchants often conceal and evade tax payments when collecting taxes on behalf of the government. Those who are caught with account books will be required to pay the total amount of evaded taxes. However, often only a portion of the invoices can be seized. Upon reviewing the account books, it is found that the amounts are not recorded, which is obviously to evade taxes. If only the discovered tax-evading invoices are used, the amount is very small. Even if they are prosecuted, it is not enough to deter the stubborn. Yesterday, the Municipal Council decided to calculate the tax based on the number of days on which the evasion was discovered, and fine them accordingly. The standard for calculating the punishment will be based on the average turnover of the largest month to rectify the banquet tax revenue.

Furthermore, in order to crack down on the unauthorized construction of sheds in the city, it was resolved that the police bureau should instruct each branch and police station to pay attention to outdoor patrols. Anyone constructing sheds without a license should be banned.

Zhongyuan Shipping Company Sues Maersk for Breach of Contract in Purchasing a Ship and Demands Compensation 61

[Report from Our Newspaper] The first Sino-British international civil lawsuit was heard in the District Court yesterday. The plaintiff in the case was Zhongyuan Shipping Company, and the defendant was the British merchant Maersk (i.e., Laisi Shipping Company). On November 28th of last year, Zhongyuan Shipping Company purchased the "Wenifu Lei Maersk" ship from the British merchant Maersk, stipulating that the ship would be delivered when it arrived in Shanghai, with a total price of 75,000 pounds. Unexpectedly, after paying in installments, the plaintiff suddenly received a notice from the defendant on March 8th of this year, requesting to terminate the contract and return the deposit of 52,000 pounds and interest of 25 pounds, 5 shillings, and 6 pence. Zhongyuan Company then requested the defendant to compensate for the losses suffered due to the failure to perform the contract in accordance with Article 260 of the Civil Code, amounting to 774,479,944 yuan in legal tender and 13,088 pounds in British currency. The defendant stated that the seller of the "Wenifu Lei Maersk" ship was originally British Maersk Co., Ltd., located in London. However, the plaintiff proved from the defendant's letters that the Maersk shipping companies in London and Shanghai were originally one company. Moreover, the contract stated that delivery was required upon the second payment. Although the defendant received the second payment, it did not deliver the ship but returned the payment, which shows the intention to terminate the contract. The defendant replied: Because the British Wartime Transportation Bureau issued a ban on the transfer of various means of transportation, the ship was not allowed to be sold. Regarding this point, the defendant was forced to do so and had sent a letter to the plaintiff stating this, so please reject the plaintiff's lawsuit. The plaintiff firmly believed that the contract stated that the delivery date was the second payment, so the sovereignty of the ship undoubtedly belonged to the plaintiff. Since the defendant had breached the contract, it was natural to request compensation for losses. At this point, the court ordered the debate to end, and the sentence was set for the morning of the 24th. If the defendant loses the case, the amount of compensation will be determined in due course.

After the Administration Headquarters Reorganizes its Structure, Materials are Speeded up for Inland Transportation; 20,000 Tons Out of 70,000 Tons of Inventory Have Been Shipped; Hope that the United Nations Relief and Rehabilitation Administration Will Withdraw its Order Soon 67

[Report from Our Newspaper] Since Liu Hongsheng, the executive director of the "Administration Headquarters", recently reorganized the agency, his authority has greatly increased. The most urgent task among his newly added tasks is to speed up the inland transportation of materials so that the director of the "United Nations Relief and Rehabilitation Administration," La Guardia, can withdraw his order soon. The LST and LSM ships managed by China Merchants Bureau, totaling about 21,000 tons, will independently bear the transportation task. According to statistics from the "Administration Headquarters," if the ban is lifted and the quantity of materials coming to China remains unchanged, then 175,000 tons of ships per month will be needed for transportation, which is far from the total tonnage currently owned by China Merchants Bureau. Therefore, some related parties are not optimistic about whether the transportation tools will be sufficient in the future and whether La Guardia's ban can be lifted soon, because these ships must also send refugees in addition to transporting materials.

Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce, Will Go to the Northeast 68

Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the National Federation of Commerce, will depart for the nine northeastern provinces at the end of this month. His task is to investigate the commercial and pharmaceutical conditions in the Northeast and assist in the establishment of provincial federations of commerce to participate in the founding meeting of the National Federation of Commerce. According to Wang, when he met with reporters yesterday, the conference is scheduled to be officially convened in the capital on November 1. Currently, provincial federations of commerce and municipal chambers of commerce are being established in turn. At that time, 43 units will participate. As for all national federations of guilds (such as the recently established Insurance Guild Federation), they will also participate and be listed as "horizontal organizations."

The United Nations Relief and Rehabilitation Administration (UNRRA) recently transported a large number of materials to China, totaling more than ten ships, which have arrived in Shanghai. Weather Forecast 70

According to the Shanghai Meteorological Observatory, the typhoon swirling in the South China Sea was still moving slowly yesterday on the sea between Shantou and Hong Kong. It then slightly turned, and the center of the vortex brushed Hong Kong in the afternoon and landed near Heshan, Guangdong at night. It moved rapidly to the northwest and has now reached Guizhou Province. Its strength has weakened and turned into a low-pressure system, gradually disappearing.

The Pacific airflow is stable in Japan, the East China Sea, and the Ryukyu Islands. Tropical airflow covers the whole country.

Weather forecast: Yellow Sea, cloudy and sunny, haze in the morning, moderate easterly to southerly wind, moderate waves.

Central China, cloudy and sunny but hot, partial cloudy, morning fog, and evening thunderstorms, variable light wind.

Shanghai: cloudy and sunny but hot, moderate southeasterly to southwesterly wind, East China Sea, cloudy and sunny, moderate southeasterly to southwesterly wind, partial coastal fog in the morning, moderate waves.

Temperature on the 19th: High 92.9 degrees, low 77.9 degrees.

Education and Sports

Vocational Education Development in Xikang Province: Dividing the Province into Six Vocational Education Zones 71

[Our Yaan Correspondent] The Education Department of Xikang Province, in order to develop vocational education, has specially divided the entire province into six vocational education zones: The first zone encompasses the counties under Yaan's jurisdiction, with the Provincial Yaan Industrial School as its center; the second vocational education zone includes the eight counties/bureaus of Xichang, Dechang, Huili, Yuejun, Mianning, Ningnan, Zhaojue, and Ningdong, with the Provincial Xichang Agricultural School as its center, and also contains the National Jinjiang Vocational School in Huili. The third vocational education zone includes the three counties of Yanyuan, Jianbian, and Jiulong, with the planned Provincial Yanyuan Junior Vocational School as its center. The fourth vocational education zone includes the three counties of Kangding, Luting, and Ba'an, with the Provincial Kangding Commercial Vocational School as its center, and also contains the Provincial Kangding Agricultural Vocational School and the Provincial Luting Vocational School. The fifth vocational education zone includes the counties/bureaus on the northern route of Xikang Province, with the planned Provincial Garze Junior Vocational School as its center. The sixth vocational education zone includes the counties on the southern route of Xikang Province, with the planned Provincial Ba'an Junior Vocational School as its center.

Peiping Normal College: Reinstating the Graduate School; Liang Shiqiu to Head the English Department 72

[Our Peiping Correspondent, 19th] Peiping Normal College has decided to reinstate the graduate school, adding a department of education in addition to the existing departments of Chinese Studies and History. Furthermore, the college has hired Liang Shiqiu to head the English Department and Ma Sicong to head the Music Department. Most of the professors are being hired from the Northwest Normal College.

Yanjing University's Restoration to its Former Grandeur: Not Easily Achieved in the Short Term; Acting President Lu Zhigong Tells Reporter 73

[Our Peiping Correspondent, 19th] Yanjing University, which is reopening in Peiping, is currently facing financial difficulties. According to Acting President Lu Zhigong, who told a reporter: Yanjing University's funding relies heavily on American donations, but due to high inflation, one US dollar is currently worth less than thirty cents in pre-war Chinese currency, so the school's income only covers one-third of its expenses, with the remaining two-thirds needing to be found domestically. The engineering college that Yanjing University planned to add this year will remain merged with the science college due to financial difficulties, with engineering courses being added to the physics and chemistry departments. Most of the school's equipment was lost after the Pacific War and has yet to be recovered. The equipment currently in use is mostly borrowed from the Peking Union Medical College Hospital. There is also a significant shortage of professors, especially in the Journalism and Economics departments, which have the largest number of students. Several American professors that Provost Stuart was planning to hire have been unable to come to China due to transportation and domestic order problems. The restoration of Yanjing University to its former grandeur will likely take one or two years to achieve.

National Jiangsu Medical College: Relocating and Reopening at the Foot of Beigu Mountain 74

[Our Zhenjiang Correspondent] The National Jiangsu Medical College, formerly the Jiangsu Provincial Medical and Political College, moved west in response to the outbreak of the Anti-Japanese War. In 1938, it was ordered by the Ministry of Education to merge with the medical department of Nantong College and was reorganized as a national institution. In 1939, it moved to northern Sichuan. In 1941, it continued to run a senior nursing school, with one class already graduated. Since the year before last, it has also offered a medical specialization program and a health education specialization program. There are currently over 400 students. Hundreds of graduates serve in medical institutions in various provinces and cities. Fortunately, most of the college's buildings remained intact during the Anti-Japanese War, but the hospital was damaged and needs to be repaired. It is reported that 20 outpatient clinics have already been built, and the remaining classrooms, laboratories, dormitories, and affiliated hospitals will be actively repaired during the reconstruction period so that they can be used. The campus is located at the foot of Beigu Mountain in Zhenjiang, covering an area of over 180 acres. Classes are expected to begin in the fall after the complete reconstruction.

Executive Yuan Approves Measures: Defining and Managing the Authority of Overseas Chinese Education 75

[Our Nanjing Correspondent] The authority in charge of overseas Chinese affairs is the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. Overseas Chinese education is jointly managed by the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission and the Ministry of Education. Recently, the Executive Yuan strengthened the efficiency of overseas Chinese education and cultural work, approving the "Measures for Defining and Managing the Authority of Overseas Chinese Education," and issuing an order to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, the Ministry of Education, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to comply. The main points of the measures are as follows: (1) Overseas Chinese education and culture are primarily managed by the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, with the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs as assisting agencies. (2) Domestic Overseas Chinese education and culture are primarily managed by the Ministry of Education, with the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission as an assisting agency. (3) Overseas Chinese education facilities that simultaneously involve domestic and foreign affairs should be managed by the agency whose business is at the core of the issue. (4) When the competent authority takes important measures regarding its managed business, it should notify the assisting agency or consult its opinion in advance. The assisting agency may make suggestions or provide assistance at any time. (5) The Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission may direct overseas embassies and consulates to exercise administrative power over overseas Chinese education and culture. (6) The budgets of various ministries and commissions related to overseas Chinese education and culture should be incorporated into the expenditure items of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, and the plans should be implemented by the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. (7) Regulations related to Overseas Chinese education and culture should be revised separately in accordance with the above provisions.

Zhejiang Education Department to Act as Agent for Naval Academy Admissions 76

[Our Hangzhou Correspondent] The Zhejiang Provincial Government has approved a dispatch from the Naval Headquarters stating that the Naval Academy will be recruiting 200 new students during the summer term this year and has entrusted the Provincial Government to act as an agent for the preliminary admissions exams. Based on population ratio, this province is entitled to select 41 candidates. Any citizen with sound credentials and pure ideology, aged between 17 and 20, and a high school graduate, may apply. Registration will begin on the 23rd of this month and end on the 27th. Physical examinations will be conducted on the 29th and 30th. Examinations will begin on August 1st.

World Education Leaders to Establish International Education Organization 77

[United States Information Service, New York, Endicott, 18th] Education leaders from around the world will gather here in August of this year to plan the establishment of an international education organization aimed at improving cultural standards and assisting in solving school problems. Education representatives from 30 countries will not represent their respective governments but will speak for their respective countries' education affairs. One important issue to be discussed is how teachers can improve international understanding and peace education. Another issue to be discussed is how to assist countries whose education systems were destroyed during the war. This conference, convened by the National Education Association, will advocate close cooperation with the United Nations Educational, Scientific and Cultural Organization.

Ministry of Education Approves Review Examinees: Permitted to Participate in Study Abroad Exams with Certification 78

The Shanghai Review Committee of the Ministry of Education, in order to safeguard the opportunity for further education for graduates of schools above the specialization level during the period of occupation, has issued certificates temporarily allowing them to take the study abroad examination. It is now reported that the case has been submitted to the Ministry of Education and approved by instruction No. 7666 of the Liu character dated July 10. The text of the Zhu instruction is as follows: "It is noted that graduates of national, enemy puppet universities and enemy puppet independent colleges are temporarily allowed to apply for the exam with the review registration certificate, but after passing the examination, they must submit a review qualification certificate before they can receive a study abroad certificate. Graduates of enemy puppet vocational schools who have not served are not allowed to apply. Please take note." It was previously reported that graduates of enemy puppet schools above the specialization level who have not been reviewed may also apply for study abroad exams directly. This must have been a misunderstanding.

This City's Elementary School Joint Advancement Association to Continue Holding the 4th Advancement Class 79

The Elementary School Joint Advancement Association, in order to enhance teachers' research interest and improve teaching effectiveness, will hold the fourth advancement class during the summer term, divided into required courses, elective courses, and summer mobile camps. Required courses will feature ten renowned professors who will lead ten education lectures, held at Yicai Middle School from 8:00 to 10:00 am on Sunday mornings and from 4:00 to 6:00 pm on Wednesday afternoons, for five consecutive weeks, totaling twenty hours. Elective courses are divided into specialized and joint courses. Specialized subjects include music, physical education, labor arts, and children's drama. Joint subjects include compound mathematics and teaching supervision, and standard language and applied writing, each with 40 hours, held every Monday, Tuesday, Thursday, Friday, and Saturday from 3:00 to 5:00 pm or 4:00 to 6:00 pm, for four consecutive weeks. The location is still under negotiation. The summer mobile camp will be held approximately four times, gathering collectively in the suburbs or parks for picnics and various recreational activities. The fee for participating in the required courses is 2,000 yuan, and the fee for elective courses is 4,000 yuan. Those who take both courses simultaneously will also pay 4,000 yuan. It is reported that the number of places is limited. Elementary school teachers who wish to participate can register at the association's headquarters at No. 1, Lane 66, Zhejiang South Road, or at the branch associations in each district.

City Education Bureau Convenes Study Abroad Examination Supervision Committee Meeting Yesterday 81

The City Education Bureau was ordered to handle the supervision of the examination for government-funded and self-funded students studying abroad. Therefore, at 3:00 PM yesterday, a meeting of the Examination Supervision Committee was held in the bureau's auditorium. More than sixty people attended, including Yu Qingtang, Zhou Feicheng, Jin Tongyin, Ma Chonggan, Ma Jingxuan, Zheng Tongsun, Song Zijing, Tang Songyuan, Cao Fengchu, Shi Peng, Chai Zifei, Wang Zunwu, and Hu Huaitian. Deputy Director Li Ximou served as chairman and carefully discussed the various matters that should be paid attention to during supervision until the meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM. The points to note for the supervision of the public and self-funded study abroad examinations and the schedule for the public-funded study abroad examinations are listed as follows:

Examination Supervision Notes

(1) The Deputy Minister of Education and members of the Examination Commission will supervise all examination rooms, and additional supervisors will be hired. (2) The examination rules are printed on the back of the admission ticket. Please check that the supervisors implement them. (3) A preparatory entrance signal will be sounded ten minutes before each exam. The entrance signal will be sounded when the exam starts, and the exit signal will be sounded when the exam ends. (4) The examination papers and questions for each examination room will be handed over to the supervisors by the supervisory personnel, who will carry them to the examination room and place the examination papers and questions on the tables according to seat number, paying attention to whether the seat number filled in on the examination paper matches the seat number on the table, and whether the examination subject matches the subject printed on the examination paper. (5) When the entrance signal sounds, the examination room door will be opened and candidates will enter. (6) Each examination room will have an examination room record sheet, which will be used by the supervisor to record whether any violations have occurred and other situations. (7) If any candidates do not arrive within ten minutes after the start of each exam, the supervisor will retrieve their examination papers and questions and note it on the examination room record sheet. (8) The supervisor will verify each candidate's examination certificate and photo in the photo album within ten minutes after the start of each exam to ensure that the photos match the candidate's appearance and that the seat number on the examination certificate and examination paper matches the seat number on the table. (9) The examination room record sheet and photo album will be the responsibility of the supervisory personnel. The supervisor will sign a receipt on the prepared examination room paper title book after receiving the responsibility. (10) If the examination paper is not enough for writing, candidates may request additional examination paper, which should be glued on. (11) The supervisor should remind the candidates of the time from time to time half an hour before the end of the exam. (12) When the candidates hand in their papers, the supervisors will cut off the floating labels on the examination paper and place them in an empty paper bag to avoid them being discarded on the floor, which would be unsightly. (13) After all the examination papers have been collected in each examination room, the supervisor will count the number of copies and seal them on the spot, indicating the examination room, subject, and number of copies, and sign and seal the seal. The unexamined papers and any extra blank papers will be sent to the examination paper supervisor for storage.

Publicly Funded Study Abroad Examination Schedule

The South China Football Team's Visit to Shanghai: Sports Association Issues Statement: Recounts the Welfare Foundation's Negotiation Process 87

The City Sports Association yesterday issued a statement regarding Li Huitang leading the South China team to Shanghai at the invitation of the China Welfare Fund to participate in charity matches. The statement recounts the negotiation process between the Welfare Association and the City Sports Association as follows:

"On the 17th, various newspapers in this city published reports that Mr. Li Huitang was invited by the China Welfare Fund Committee to lead the South China Football Team to Shanghai to participate in charity football matches. In order to be cautious, the association deems it necessary to recount the negotiation process. In late June, a sports news report in a certain newspaper stated that Mrs. Sun had initiated the invitation to Mr. Li Huitang to lead the team to Shanghai to hold charity football matches, and the preparations were reported in the newspapers from time to time. On the 2nd of this month, the China Welfare Fund Committee sent a representative, Ms. Tan Liuqingxuan, with a letter to Zhou Jiaqi of the Football Committee, stating that they planned to hold charity football matches in mid-month in order to raise funds for disaster relief, and they had invited Mr. Li Huitang of the South China Football Team to preside over the matches. They requested assistance in inviting the participating teams, referees, and organizing the match schedule. Mr. Zhou Jiaqi replied with the reasons for holding the matches in late August, citing that the football season had ended and the various difficulties of holding them at an unsuitable time. On the 12th of this month, the Football Committee received a second letter from the China Welfare Fund Committee, which briefly stated: "Disaster relief is as urgent as putting out a fire. The South China team has decided to come to Shanghai and is preparing to depart. In order to alleviate the various difficulties of your association (Football Committee), the Welfare Foundation has contacted various teams and related parties and has been kindly promised support and assistance. Therefore, as soon as the South China team arrives in port in the coming days, our association will decide on the match date and ask for your guidance and full assistance." The Football Committee of the Sports Association, because this matter concerned the duties of the association, submitted it to the Council of Directors for discussion. At the meeting held at 2:00 PM on the 13th of this month, the two letters sent by the China Welfare Fund Committee to the Football Committee regarding the proposed hosting of the South China football team's visit to Shanghai to participate in charity matches were submitted. The decision was made that: (1) According to Article 3 of the Regulations for Sports Competitions Organized by Municipal Mass Organizations established by this association, "Municipal mass organizations that wish to raise charitable funds by holding public competitions and issuing tickets must obtain prior approval from this association before publicly selling tickets." (2) The football season has passed. Based on the above two points, it is difficult to comply. The aforementioned decision was sent to the Welfare Foundation for their review on the 15th of this month. After Li Huitang and others arrived in Shanghai, the association also notified the South China Football Team of the resolution of the Council of Directors at noon on the 17th, and because the team members are all amateur athletes, the association hoped that they would respect the resolution of the association's Council of Directors. Fearing that various circles are not aware of the true situation of the negotiations, this is specially declared as above, in the hope that all parties will be aware."

Civil Affairs Briefs

23rd District Negotiates with Highway Bureau: Allocating Buses to Run on Songhu Line: Will Stop Once Railway is Restored 90

The traffic between Wusong Town, which belongs to the jurisdiction of the 23rd District (Wusong) of this city, and Shanghai used to be maintained by the railway. Since the road was destroyed by the enemy, it has been cut off. After the victory, although local gentry and merchants have repeatedly appealed to the two road management express runs to restore the route, the bureau has been unable to realize it due to a lack of materials, and it is still blocked, causing inconvenience to merchants and travelers. Yin Gongtian, chairman of the District People's Congress of the district, and others, in view of the need to restore transportation in order to prosper the market, initiated the organization of the Wusong Transportation Promotion Association, and have negotiated with the Directorate General of Public Roads of the Ministry of Communications to sign a contract to dispatch a number of buses to run on the Wusong-Shanghai public bus line to maintain transportation. It will be stopped once the railway is restored. The district office has been asked to submit it to the Public Utilities Bureau for approval.

Ministry of Interior Issues "Household Registration Regulations: Questions and Answers" to be Published in This Newspaper Starting Tomorrow. 91

The Ministry of Interior, to facilitate the investigation and explanation of difficult household registration issues, previously compiled the first volume of "Household Registration Regulations: Questions and Answers," which was distributed to provinces and cities for reference. It is now learned that the ministry has recently compiled the second volume of "Household Registration Regulations: Questions and Answers" based on responses to inquiries from the governments of Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Guangdong, Guangxi, Fujian, Henan, Shaanxi, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Hunan provinces, as well as the Zhejiang Civil Affairs Department, the Hunan Xiangxi Administrative Office's Compensation Committee, and inquiries and answers raised at the Joint Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai provinces political supervision conference. This second volume will be reprinted together with the first volume. Except for concentrated answers that conflict with the amended and promulgated household registration law, the non-conflicting parts still apply. All the answers from the first and second volumes will be continuously published in this newspaper starting tomorrow. It is hoped that personnel handling household registration at all levels will pay attention.

Sixth Bao of the Fourteenth District Appeals for Refugees 92

The refugees from northern Jiangsu residing between Datong Road and Gonghe Road in the Sixth Bao of the Fourteenth District of this city previously faced the imminent demolition of their thatched huts due to the Railway Bureau's road property reorganization, causing widespread fear. They jointly submitted a request for a delay last month. The Railway Bureau distributed a method requiring them to demolish the houses occupying road property themselves within one month. The refugees, still with nowhere to go, gathered at the local Bao office, requesting assistance in appealing to the Railway Bureau to convey their plight and postpone the demolition of the thatched huts. The Bao heads, Feng Dianbao and Xu Peixin, specially invited district representatives to draft a proposal, requesting the Railway Bureau to postpone the unconditional demolition for two years. They are currently awaiting a reply.

Answers to Household Registration Questions 94

Question: How do I apply for household registration for a newborn child?

Answer: For a newborn infant, you only need to apply for birth registration; it is not necessary to apply separately for household registration. Within fifteen days of the birth, obtain a birth registration application form from the local Bao office or District Office and fill it out completely. In the "Explanation of Registration Matters" section of the application form, you should write "Birth registration, (year) (month) (day)." The procedure for registering household registration due to marriage, divorce, recognition, adoption, or termination of recognition or adoption is the same.

Question: If I intend to reside in Shanghai permanently and want to establish household registration here, what are the application procedures?

Answer: Within fifteen days of moving in, fill out a household registration application form, stating the names of those who are also registering their household registration, and submit it to the local Bao office for registration. In the "Explanation of Registration Matters" section of the household registration application form, state "Permanent household registration, moved in on (year) (month) (day)."

Question: What are the procedures for foreigners who have obtained Chinese nationality to apply for household registration?

Answer: Within fifteen days after obtaining permission for Chinese nationality, the parent or the person concerned should fill in the application form with the family members who have obtained Chinese nationality together, and submit it along with the naturalization permit to the local Bao office for registration. In the "Explanation of Registration Matters" section of the application, state "Household registration, date of obtaining nationality (year) (month) (day)."

In recent days, residents of the district have been enthusiastically subscribing for shares to join the society. District Head Hou Jiyuan and Deputy District Head Wu Guanrong attended the meeting to provide guidance and discuss the society's development in detail.

Regarding the work of re-checking household registrations in the Ninth District Office, District Head Yao Cheng and Deputy District Head Wang Zikui have supervised the responsible personnel to actively handle the matter. A large part has been completed and the entire task is expected to be finished by the end of this month.

The Eighteenth District Office held a review meeting for Bao secretaries at 10:00 AM on the 15th of this month. Chairman Chang, the deputy district head, listened to reports from each Bao secretary on the progress of their work and, after questions were raised, provided instructions and explanations item by item.
